            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

</p><p><b>Pedro of the Treetops</b> was a jaguar <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">mink</a> and captain of the <a href="/wiki/Guardians" title="Guardians">Guardians</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Infobox_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Infobox-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He was the former <a href="/wiki/Captain" class="mw-redirect" title="Captain">captain</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Nox_Pirates" title="Nox Pirates">Nox Pirates</a> who sailed in search of a <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">Poneglyph</a>, and he earned a bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>382,000,000 in the process, but his journey was cut short in <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Pirate_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pirate-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> He returned to Totto Land to accompany the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates#Crew_Members" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Sanji Retrieval Team</a> in their quest to rescue <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Team_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Team-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> During the escape from Whole Cake Island, Pedro sacrificed himself to ensure his team's escape, as he believed the Straw Hats will bring about the <a href="/wiki/Dawn_of_the_World" title="Dawn of the World">Dawn of the World</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c877_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c877-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span></h2>
<p>Pedro was a large,<sup id="cite_ref-Infobox_4-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Infobox-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> male feline mink with spotted fur, white ears, and long, wavy blonde hair.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> He gave up his left eye to <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a> during his time as a pirate captain,<sup id="cite_ref-Fight_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fight-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> and afterwards covered his scar with his hair.<sup id="cite_ref-Tamago_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tamago-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> He also had a torn left ear.<sup id="cite_ref-Fight_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fight-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Upon entering <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>, Pedro donned a dress shirt with floral-like frills down the middle, a dark cape with the same frills on the edge, and a large dark hat which partially obscures his face.<sup id="cite_ref-Recognition_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Recognition-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> When meeting with the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Tank_Pirates" title="Fire Tank Pirates">Fire Tank Pirates</a>, he wore a green suit with a black shirt and a red ascot along with a green fedora.<sup id="cite_ref-c858_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c858-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a1/Pedro_Threatens_Pudding.png/revision/latest?cb=20170507183535" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Threatens Pudding" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="144" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pedro Threatens Pudding.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Threatens_Pudding.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a1/Pedro_Threatens_Pudding.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170507183535" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a1/Pedro_Threatens_Pudding.png/revision/latest?cb=20170507183535" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Threatens Pudding" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a1/Pedro_Threatens_Pudding.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170507183535" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="144" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pedro Threatens Pudding.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Threatens_Pudding.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a1/Pedro_Threatens_Pudding.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170507183535" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pedro_Threatens_Pudding.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro threatens Pudding.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Pedro was extremely loyal to whomever he follows, and was often overly eager to use violence to help his allies during tense situations without waiting for discussion.<sup id="cite_ref-c826_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c826-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c827_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c827-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c828_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c828-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> As a Guardian, he was willing to lay down his life in order to defend the Whale Forest against intruders, though he admitted that he and the rest of the Guardians are a bit too sensitive to intruders,<sup id="cite_ref-Infobox_4-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Infobox-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> and would call off an attack if asked to do so.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> However, when not on duty as a Guardian, Pedro could be very cautious and distrusting toward strangers, quickly preparing to use force against anyone he feels may be a threat to him and his friends even if they seem to be friendly, as demonstrated during his first encounter with <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Pudding" title="Charlotte Pudding">Charlotte Pudding</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c828_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c828-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He seemed to like standing in trees and other high places, as fitting for his nickname,<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Infobox_4-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Infobox-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Jump_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jump-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c823_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c823-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> and was sometimes intense when he got up close to people.<sup id="cite_ref-Press_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Press-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>According to <a href="/wiki/Tamago" title="Tamago">Tamago</a>, Pedro used to highly prioritize his own survival when he was a pirate captain.<sup id="cite_ref-Tamago_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tamago-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> He willingly gave up his left eye in order to prove to <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a> that he needed to return to <a href="/wiki/Zou" title="Zou">Zou</a> alive and witness "the <a href="/wiki/Dawn_of_the_World" title="Dawn of the World">dawn of the world</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-Fight_10-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fight-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Pedro believed this dream has come to fruition with the Straw Hats, so he was fine with dying as soon as his obligations to the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hats</a> were fulfilled.<sup id="cite_ref-Fight_10-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fight-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> As a result, he became a rather reckless fighter willing to go great lengths against enemies due to his lack of regard for his own safety.
</p><p>He was also very perceptive and cautious; he was the only member of the Sanji Retrieval Team to be suspicious of Charlotte Pudding's motives due to her connection to Big Mom,<sup id="cite_ref-c828_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c828-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> which was later proven correct.<sup id="cite_ref-Fight_10-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fight-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He also berated <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a> for stowing away on the journey to Totto Land, reminding her of the danger they were heading into.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Allies">Allies</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Mink_Tribe">Mink Tribe</span></h4>
<p>Pedro cared about <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a>, going as far as to beg the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> to save them despite being near death himself.<sup id="cite_ref-c810_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c810-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> He also seemed to have a rivalry with the Captain of the <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi_Musketeer_Squad" title="Inuarashi Musketeer Squad">Musketeers</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shishilian" title="Shishilian">Shishilian</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Team_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Team-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He is well respected among the citizens who admire his strength. Even members of the tribe that live elsewhere are shown to respect him.<sup id="cite_ref-Recognition_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Recognition-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When learning of his demise, they built a grave marker for him on <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>, with Wanda, Shishilian, and Carrot honoring him.<sup id="cite_ref-c955_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c955-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later at <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, when Nekomamushi learned about Pedro's death and that <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a>, the one responsible for Pedro's death was nearby, an angry Nekomamushi headed after Perospero, determined to avenge his comrade's death.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> After he and Shishilian found him, Nekomamushi attacked Perospero.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> and was eventually able to defeat him to avenge Pedro.<sup id="cite_ref-c1026_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1026-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pekoms">Pekoms</span></h4>
<p>Pedro and Pekoms were sworn brothers, and both have an extremely strong bond as Pedro was the only one who could calm Pekoms's mindless rampage in his Sulong form. They once sailed together as the Nox Pirates. Pekoms later left the crew, but after Pedro and Zepo's defeat at Totto Land, Pekoms begged for Pedro's life to be spared, proving that he cared about Pedro.<sup id="cite_ref-Fight_10-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fight-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> When he heard about Pedro's death, he grieved greatly, and was willing to carry on Pedro's will even though it meant going against his crew.<sup id="cite_ref-c882_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c882-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Although they were very close, Pekoms seemed to fear Pedro slightly, as he grew nervous when the two of them reunited on Zou and Nekomamushi stated that Pedro was the only one capable of keeping him under control.<sup id="cite_ref-Team_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Team-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zepo">Zepo</span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Zepo" title="Zepo">Zepo</a> was a member of the <a href="/wiki/Nox_Pirates" title="Nox Pirates">Nox Pirates</a> under Pedro. They had a good friendship, since Zepo was the only one who remained with Pedro in the crew while the others left due to a drop in morale. When Zepo died after giving up his lifespan to Big Mom, Pedro cried over his loss. Even when gouging out his left eye to survive, the jaguar mink was still tearing up for Zepo.<sup id="cite_ref-Fight_10-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fight-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Carrot">Carrot</span></h4>
<p>As a fellow mink, Pedro got along very well with <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a>. In the past, he was the one who gave her gauntlets after he witnessed her lack of talent for <a href="/wiki/Sword" title="Sword">swordsmanship</a>. He then repeated the words <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a> told him in his youth to encourage her to become stronger.<sup id="cite_ref-Carrot_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Carrot-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> When he found out that Carrot snuck aboard the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>, he was worried about her and asked to turn around to bring her back, but after Luffy agreed to let her stay, he commented about her strength, showing a protective yet proud attitude towards her.<sup id="cite_ref-c823_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c823-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Pedro planned to sacrifice himself for the escape of the Sanji Retrieval Team, he warned Carrot beforehand, expressing his desire for their survival.<sup id="cite_ref-c877_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c877-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> After his presumable death, Carrot was brought to tears and tried to rush over to him, only to be stopped by <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>. She later charged towards <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Katakuri" title="Charlotte Katakuri">Charlotte Katakuri</a> in her grief.<sup id="cite_ref-Carrot_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Carrot-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span></h4>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> and his group first arrived on Zou, Pedro realized they were not with Jack and begged them to save Inuarashi and Nekomamushi.<sup id="cite_ref-c810_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c810-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> He later defended them from a misguided and belligerent <a href="/wiki/Wanda" title="Wanda">Wanda</a> by revealing that they were there to help.<sup id="cite_ref-Defending_Straw_Hats_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Defending_Straw_Hats-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> When <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> arrived several days later and entered the Whale Forest without permission, Pedro had the Guardians surround him with the intent to attack, but ordered everyone to retreat after Wanda told him to.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> When he met the Straw Hats later that night, he apologized for attacking Luffy earlier and thanked them for saving the minks' lives.<sup id="cite_ref-Press_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Press-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to Sanji's efforts to help save him and his people, Pedro was very fond of Sanji and was extremely eager and willing to assist the Straw Hats in rescuing him from Big Mom's captivity.<sup id="cite_ref-Press_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Press-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Per his request, he joined Luffy's Sanji Retrieval Team in order to fulfill his gratitude.<sup id="cite_ref-Team_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Team-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Pedro and Brook worked well together, with Pedro trusting the other to get the rubbings of the <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">Poneglyphs</a> while he served as a distraction.<sup id="cite_ref-Plan_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Plan-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Pedro later took part in freeing the musician from Big Mom's clutches. When reunited, Pedro was surprised that Brook was successful in his mission even though they faced many risks in completing it.<sup id="cite_ref-c855_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c855-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Believing that the Straw Hats are the people who would lead the world to a new dawn, Pedro was willing to sacrifice his own life for them. During the escape from Whole Cake Island, he attempted to take down Perospero with a suicidal explosion in order to ensure the Straw Hats escape.<sup id="cite_ref-c877_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c877-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Though Perospero survived the explosion, Pedro's actions freed his friends and the Sunny, allowing them to escape. The team then grieved over Pedro's death afterwards.<sup id="cite_ref-Carrot_28-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Carrot-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Government">World Government</span></h4>
<p>As a former notorious pirate captain of the <a href="/wiki/Nox_Pirates" title="Nox Pirates">Nox Pirates</a>, Pedro was an enemy of the World Government. Despite his intention of being a mere explorer, the government nevertheless placed a bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>382,000,000 on his head.<sup id="cite_ref-Pirate_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pirate-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Fight_10-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fight-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Big_Mom_Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</span></h4>
<p>After he first entered Totto Land as captain of the Nox Pirates, he clashed with the Big Mom Pirates during his search for Poneglyphs. After his defeat, Big Mom was prepared to take 70 years of his lifespan after Zepo reached the "100 years of lifespan" on her roulette and died after losing 30 years. However, with Pekoms' pleading and Pedro gouging out his own left eye as compensation for Tamago's lost eye, Big Mom was impressed and reduced the amount taken to 50 years, allowing Pedro to return to Zou alive.<sup id="cite_ref-Tamago_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tamago-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Five years later, he returned to Totto Land with the Sanji Retrieval Team and once again fought against them to help obtain their Poneglyphs. Pedro distrusted <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Pudding" title="Charlotte Pudding">Charlotte Pudding</a> because she is Big Mom's daughter, and suggested they restrain her, and his suspicions were initially correct as she was initially indeed an enemy.<sup id="cite_ref-c828_18-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c828-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> During the tea party, Charlotte Oven remembered Pedro from his past invasion and swore that he would not leave alive this time.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He was familiar with <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Perospero</a>, as the latter escorted him out of Big Mom's territory after his first failed invasion five years ago. Perospero mocked Pedro on his invasion and shortened lifespan.<sup id="cite_ref-flashback_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-flashback-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> They met again during the Sanji Retrieval Team's invasion and briefly fought. With Perospero trapping his allies, Pedro blew himself up to take him out. He was unsuccessful in killing Perospero, although his sacrifice did allow the Sanji Retrieval Team to escape from Perospero, and he cursed Pedro afterward, wanting to go after Pedro's allies for revenge.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Despite Pedro's sacrifice, during the Fire Festival in Wano Country, Perospero was attacked by Pedro's Mink Tribe comrades who wanted to avenge his death, first by Carrot and Wanda, and later by the Mink Tribe leader Nekomamushi, with the latter succeeding despite taking some heavy injures earlier in the process. <sup id="cite_ref-c1026_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1026-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Tamago">Tamago</span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Despite being enemies, I've always respected you as a powerful opponent, Pedro, captain of the Nox Pirates! Every time we would see each other, the scars on our left eyes would both begin to itch!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;<a href="/wiki/Tamago" title="Tamago">Tamago</a><sup id="cite_ref-Tamago_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tamago-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p>During his time as a pirate captain, Pedro clashed with Tamago on at least one occasion, resulting in the loss of Tamago's left eye. Despite this, Tamago has always respected Pedro as a powerful opponent.<sup id="cite_ref-Tamago_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tamago-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> While Pedro's attitude toward Tamago is unknown, his actions against him did not indicate respect as he went to great measures to try to annihilate Tamago, and he was unwilling to sacrifice his life against him due to his obligations to the Straw Hats.<sup id="cite_ref-c853_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c853-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Pedro sacrificed himself to help his team escape Whole Cake Island, Tamago seemed to have respect for Pedro's noble intentions. Furthermore, Pedro's self sacrifice gave him a new perspective of the Straw Hats.<sup id="cite_ref-c882_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c882-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other">Other</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gol_D._Roger">Gol D. Roger</span></h4>
<p>The late <a href="/wiki/Pirate#The_King_of_Pirates" title="Pirate">Pirate King</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, visited <a href="/wiki/Zou" title="Zou">Zou</a> sometime during Pedro's childhood. After meeting the ambitious young <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">mink</a>, Roger declined his request to join his travels with <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a> but comforted him, saying that his time would come.
</p><p>When Pedro learned about Roger's death from <a href="/wiki/Wanda" title="Wanda">Wanda</a>, he was shocked by the news.<sup id="cite_ref-flashback_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-flashback-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Sometime later during <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a>'s training, he repeated Roger's words to her to encourage her to become stronger despite her lack of <a href="/wiki/Sword" title="Sword">swordsmanship</a> skills, and gave her her gauntlets instead.
</p><p>His relationship with Roger was similar to <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>' as they asked to join the latter's crew but were rejected, prompting them to start their own journey to follow their dreams.<sup id="cite_ref-flashback_8-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-flashback-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span></h2>
<p>As the captain of the <a href="/wiki/Guardians" title="Guardians">Guardians</a>, Pedro had command over them,<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> though his position and authority were below those of <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Guardian_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Guardian-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> He also had full command over the <a href="/wiki/Nox_Pirates" title="Nox Pirates">Nox Pirates</a> as their captain until they were defeated and dissolved. Nonetheless, the World Government acknowledged his strength and threat as a pirate, enough to have a <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>382,000,000 bounty placed on his head.<sup id="cite_ref-Fight_10-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fight-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Having traveled through the seas in search of <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">Poneglyphs</a>, Pedro was experienced and knowledgeable of various facts, such as the geography of <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a> and the hierarchy and powers of the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Pirate_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pirate-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Pedro was shown to possess a strong will as he was able to withstand a burst of Big Mom's <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c865_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c865-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tactical_Skills">Tactical Skills</span></h3>
<p>Pedro was very pragmatic in battle, using a large variety of battle tactics and weapons and going to great lengths in order to attain victory, disregarding any code of honor. Pedro would even attack his opponent if they were down but still had a chance of returning for battle.<sup id="cite_ref-c853_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c853-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> His ingenuity and deception was further shown when he created a massive explosion to annihilate his enemies while appearing to commit suicide when in reality, he escaped <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">into a nearby mirror</a> through <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Brûlée</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> <a href="/wiki/Mira_Mira_no_Mi" title="Mira Mira no Mi">powers</a>, deceiving the Big Mom Pirates including the intelligent Niwatori to think he was dead.<sup id="cite_ref-c853_35-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c853-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Electro" title="Electro">Electro</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>As the captain of the Guardians, Pedro was an extremely powerful warrior even for a mink and could use <a href="/wiki/Electro" title="Electro">Electro</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Fight_10-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fight-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> He had tremendous tolerance to pain, having gouged out his left eye with only slight discomfort, and also stood up after being <a href="/wiki/Koro" title="Koro">poisoned</a> and tortured by Jack, who tortured only the strongest mink warriors.<sup id="cite_ref-c810_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c810-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Defending_Straw_Hats_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Defending_Straw_Hats-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> He could also jump to great heights from a standing position.<sup id="cite_ref-Jump_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jump-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He was very stealthy, as <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>, a proficient <a href="/wiki/Observation_Haki" class="mw-redirect" title="Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a> user, did not sense him hiding in the trees above him.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> His great stealth capabilities allowed him to sneak inside a Biscuit Soldier together with Brook and also to eavesdrop on Tamago without the latter noticing. He was also extremely fast and agile, allowing him to run on walls. He used this speed in conjunction with his swordsmanship to unleash hit-and-run attacks on opponents.<sup id="cite_ref-Blitz_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blitz-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> During his fight against Tamago, he was shown able to spin his tail to use it as a helicopter to float and move in mid-air.<sup id="cite_ref-Fight_10-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fight-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Swordsmanship">Swordsmanship</span></h3>
<p>Pedro was shown to be an extremely skilled swordsman, as his sword swings are powerful enough to break through shields and armor, and he often attacked while running past his enemies rather than in a conventional manner.<sup id="cite_ref-Blitz_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blitz-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> His swordsmanship was great enough to fight on par with Tamago, a powerful member of the Big Mom Pirates, and he managed to cut Tamago's eye in one of their battles as well as defeat two of <a href="/wiki/Tama_Tama_no_Mi" title="Tama Tama no Mi">his forms</a> in their final battle.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_Only_Attacks">Anime Only Attacks</span></h4>
<ul><li><b>Juken: Karajishi</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>獣剣唐獅子</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>じゅうけんからじし</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Jūken Karajishi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Beast Sword: Imperial Guardian Lion")</span>: an anime-only sword technique, used by Pedro in the Seducing Woods.<span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources." style="text-decoration: underline dotted;"></span><sup>[<a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Wiki:Guidebook/Referencing_Information" title="One Piece Wiki:Guidebook/Referencing Information">citation needed</a>]</sup>In the Funimation adaptations, this is called <b>Beast Sword Karajishi</b>.</li></ul>
