</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 222px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 222px; height: 222px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Pedro%27s_Swordsmanship.png/revision/latest?cb=20171112021502" class="image"><img alt="Pedro&#39;s Swordsmanship" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" data-image-name="Pedro&#39;s Swordsmanship.png" data-image-key="Pedro%27s_Swordsmanship.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Pedro%27s_Swordsmanship.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20171112021502" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Pedro's hit-and-run style with his rapier.
</div></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span></h3>
<p>To utilize his swordsmanship, Pedro wielded a variety of bladed weapons. During the battle with the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> on Zou, Pedro wielded a large machete.<sup id="cite_ref-Guardian_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Guardian-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Upon his departure from Zou and during the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island_Arc" title="Whole Cake Island Arc">Whole Cake Island Arc</a>, he wielded a rapier.<sup id="cite_ref-Team_11-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Team-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Explosive_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20200911095503" class="image"><img alt="Explosive Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="149" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Explosive Infobox.png" data-image-key="Explosive_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Explosive_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200911095503" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Explosive_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20200911095503" class="image"><img alt="Explosive Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Explosive_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200911095503" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="149" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Explosive Infobox.png" data-image-key="Explosive_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Explosive_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200911095503" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Explosive_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro sets off his stockpile of explosives.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Pedro possessed a large stockpile of dynamite-shaped explosives, which he kept inside his jacket while in Totto Land. He used a single stick in order to cause a hit-and-run explosion in the Whole Cake Chateau hallways,<sup id="cite_ref-Blitz_38-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blitz-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> and later detonated several on the third floor courtyard to annihilate a large horde of enemies with a massive explosion, which acted as a smokescreen as he escaped into the <a href="/wiki/Mirror_World" class="mw-redirect" title="Mirror World">Mirror World</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c853_35-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c853-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> He later lit up the stash in his jacket which caused a massive explosion that engulfed both Perospero and himself, and even though it did not harm Big Mom, it was powerful enough to hurl her several feet away.<sup id="cite_ref-c877_12-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c877-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Pedro possessed the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament</a> and <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Childhood">Childhood</span></h4>
<p>26 years ago, when the <a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a> visited <a href="/wiki/Zou" title="Zou">Zou</a>, Pedro asked to accompany <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>. However, Roger told Pedro to remain on Zou but also told him that he would get his moment to shine one day. Pedro was later informed of Roger's execution by <a href="/wiki/Wanda" title="Wanda">Wanda</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Pirate_5-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pirate-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-flashback_8-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-flashback-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Captain_of_the_Nox_Pirates">Captain of the Nox Pirates</span></h4>
<p>13 years before the start of the series, Pedro captained the <a href="/wiki/Nox_Pirates" title="Nox Pirates">Nox Expedition Party</a> in search of a <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">Poneglyph</a>. Despite his intention of being only an explorer, the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> nevertheless placed a <a href="/wiki/Bounties" title="Bounties">bounty</a> on his head, thus the group being renamed the "Nox Pirates". Eventually, the crew gained injuries and lost morale, so <a href="/wiki/Pekoms" title="Pekoms">Pekoms</a> took those who could not continue away, leaving only Pedro and <a href="/wiki/Zepo" title="Zepo">Zepo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Pirate_5-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pirate-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8d/Pedro_Holding_His_Eye.png/revision/latest?cb=20171203031547" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Holding His Eye" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pedro Holding His Eye.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Holding_His_Eye.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8d/Pedro_Holding_His_Eye.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171203031547" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8d/Pedro_Holding_His_Eye.png/revision/latest?cb=20171203031547" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Holding His Eye" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8d/Pedro_Holding_His_Eye.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171203031547" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pedro Holding His Eye.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Holding_His_Eye.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8d/Pedro_Holding_His_Eye.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171203031547" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pedro_Holding_His_Eye.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro offering his eye to Big Mom.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>10 years after they first started sailing, Pedro and Zepo sailed into <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a> and they reunited with Pekoms, who had joined the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a>. During their mission to steal <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>'s Road Poneglyph, Pedro clashed with <a href="/wiki/Tamago" title="Tamago">Tamago</a><sup id="cite_ref-Tamago_3-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tamago-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> and took out his left eye. Eventually, Pedro and Zepo were overwhelmed by the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a>'s crew. While facing judgment from Big Mom, Pedro's comrade Zepo landed the "100 Years of Life" option on Big Mom's roulette wheel and was killed by the <a href="/wiki/Soru_Soru_no_Mi" title="Soru Soru no Mi">loss of 30 years</a>. Pedro was faced with losing 70 years, but Pekoms' pleading convinced Big Mom to reduce it to 60 years. Pedro took out his own left eye to prove that he needed to return to Zou alive in order to witness the coming of a new dawn. Big Mom decided to reduce his taken lifespan to 50 years out of respect for his will.<sup id="cite_ref-Fight_10-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fight-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Afterwards, Pedro was handcuffed and escorted out of Totto Land along with his ship by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a>, who commented on the meaning of the name "Nox Pirates". Pedro responded by saying that "night" has the same meaning as "just before dawn".<sup id="cite_ref-flashback_8-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-flashback-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime after his return to Zou, Pedro watched a young <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a> training in swordsmanship under <a href="/wiki/Shishilian" title="Shishilian">Shishilian</a>. Pedro commented that Carrot was not suited for a sword, much to Shishilian's annoyance, and later gave Carrot her gauntlets.<sup id="cite_ref-Carrot_28-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Carrot-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Jack.27s_Invasion"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Jack's_Invasion">Jack's Invasion</span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/98/Guardians_Rush_Into_Battle.png/revision/latest?cb=20161012013517" class="image"><img alt="Guardians Rush Into Battle" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Guardians Rush Into Battle.png" data-image-key="Guardians_Rush_Into_Battle.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/98/Guardians_Rush_Into_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161012013517" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/98/Guardians_Rush_Into_Battle.png/revision/latest?cb=20161012013517" class="image"><img alt="Guardians Rush Into Battle" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/98/Guardians_Rush_Into_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161012013517" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Guardians Rush Into Battle.png" data-image-key="Guardians_Rush_Into_Battle.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/98/Guardians_Rush_Into_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161012013517" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Guardians_Rush_Into_Battle.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro and the Guardians charge to battle Jack.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>, led by <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>, invaded Zou in search of <a href="/wiki/Raizo" title="Raizo">Raizo</a>, Pedro and the other <a href="/wiki/Guardians" title="Guardians">Guardians</a> fought against them.<sup id="cite_ref-Guardian_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Guardian-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> The battle against the Beast Pirates lasted for five days. On the fifth day of the battle, Jack lost his patience and unleashed <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Koro" title="Koro">Koro</a> gas, which left the <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">Mink Tribe</a> poisoned and drastically weakened. The following day, Jack left Zou after hearing about <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Doflamingo</a>'s defeat and capture.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>'s group arrived, Pedro noticed that they were not allies of Jack and begged them to save <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c810_22-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c810-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> After Caesar neutralized the poison gas, Pedro and <a href="/wiki/Tristan" title="Tristan">Tristan</a> stopped Wanda from attacking <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> by revealing that she and her group were not the enemy. Soon afterwards, the minks were saved when Sanji's group tended to their injuries.<sup id="cite_ref-Defending_Straw_Hats_29-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Defending_Straw_Hats-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zou_Arc">Zou Arc</span></h4>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> entered the <a href="/wiki/Zou#Whale_Forest" title="Zou">Whale Forest</a>, Pedro and the other Guardians surrounded him, while <a href="/wiki/Roddy" title="Roddy">Roddy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Blackback" title="Blackback">Blackback</a> confronted him. However, when Wanda came and stopped the attack while telling him to give the order to retreat, Pedro did so, causing the rest of the Guardians to leave.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Pedro_Meets_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20161121001906" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Meets Luffy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="122" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pedro Meets Luffy.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Meets_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Pedro_Meets_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161121001906" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Pedro_Meets_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20161121001906" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Meets Luffy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Pedro_Meets_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161121001906" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="122" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pedro Meets Luffy.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Meets_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Pedro_Meets_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161121001906" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pedro_Meets_Luffy.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro offers the Guardians' help in rescuing Sanji.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>That night, when the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> returned to the Whale Forest after visiting Inuarashi, Pedro greeted them and apologized to Luffy about his men's blunder earlier before informing him that <a href="/wiki/Bepo" title="Bepo">Bepo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Heart_Pirates" title="Heart Pirates">his group</a> were waiting, though Luffy wanted to meet Nekomamushi and Pekoms. After pressing himself against Luffy, Pedro whispered the location of Pekoms and his knowledge of Sanji's predicament to him before taking Luffy to see Pekoms.<sup id="cite_ref-Infobox_4-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Infobox-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Press_21-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Press-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The next day, as <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">Kanjuro</a> entered Zou, Pedro took part in the search for them by surveying Kurau City from the top of a building. Upon seeing Inuarashi below, he tried to warn Nekomamushi to retreat temporarily, but the latter did not understand why he should do so and ended up making eye contact with Inuarashi, causing the two of them to clash. However, when the <a href="/wiki/Samurai" title="Samurai">samurais</a> revealed themselves, Pedro and the minks welcomed them and revealed that Raizo was safe on Zou before standing proudly at having kept his presence a secret.<sup id="cite_ref-Jump_19-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jump-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kin'emon showed Pedro and the other minks the crest of the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a> on his back to confirm his allegiance. When Inuarashi and Nekomamushi reluctantly called a truce for the sake of <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</a>, whom they recognized as their lord, Pedro and the rest of the minks were overjoyed.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Inuarashi and Nekomamushi took <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Law</a>, the Straw Hats, and the samurais to the Whale Tree, the minks discussed the day that the two rulers began hating each other, with Pedro noting that their feud started after they returned from their voyage with <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a> barely alive. Happy that the two rulers finally made peace with each other, Pedro and the rest of the minks began to prepare a banquet to celebrate the occasion.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Heads_Out.png/revision/latest?cb=20170529031615" class="image"><img alt="Sanji Retrieval Team Heads Out" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="206" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sanji Retrieval Team Heads Out.png" data-image-key="Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Heads_Out.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Heads_Out.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170529031615" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Heads_Out.png/revision/latest?cb=20170529031615" class="image"><img alt="Sanji Retrieval Team Heads Out" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Heads_Out.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170529031615" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="206" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sanji Retrieval Team Heads Out.png" data-image-key="Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Heads_Out.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Heads_Out.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170529031615" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Heads_Out.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro heads out with the Sanji Retrieval Team and Pekoms.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, when Inuarashi, Nekomamushi, the samurais, and the pirates returned from the Whale Tree with Raizo, Zou began shaking as <a href="/wiki/Zunesha" title="Zunesha">Zunesha</a> started crying out, throwing Pedro and the others into a state of panic.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Jack had returned and was attempting to destroy Zou by killing Zunesha. When Luffy and Momonosuke heard a majestic voice in their heads, Pedro noted that both Oden and <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a> had heard the same voice, but could not converse with it. After Zunesha retaliated on Momonosuke's command and sank Jack's fleet with one blow, Pedro and the others calmed down.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, Pedro volunteered to join the Sanji Retrieval Team, which prompted several other minks to volunteer for various reasons, to his surprise and irritation. However, Nekomamushi allowed only Pedro to accompany Luffy's group because he could keep Pekoms in line. As the team departed from Zou, everyone was shocked when Luffy jumped off Zunesha with the rest of the retrieval team.<sup id="cite_ref-Team_11-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Team-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After sailing far away from Zou on the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>, a beleaguered Pedro was shocked to see <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a> had sneaked aboard. Pedro tried to have the ship turn around, but Carrot begged them to let her come along, despite his insistence that infiltrating an Emperor's stronghold would not be a game. As Luffy permitted Carrot to stay, Pedro received a newspaper that revealed the discovery and destruction of <a href="/wiki/Baltigo" title="Baltigo">Baltigo</a>, the headquarters of the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c823_20-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c823-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5a/Random_Curry.png/revision/latest?cb=20170305182728" class="image"><img alt="Random Curry" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="59" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Random Curry.png" data-image-key="Random_Curry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5a/Random_Curry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170305182728" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5a/Random_Curry.png/revision/latest?cb=20170305182728" class="image"><img alt="Random Curry" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5a/Random_Curry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170305182728" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="59" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Random Curry.png" data-image-key="Random_Curry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5a/Random_Curry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170305182728" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Random_Curry.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Sanji Retrieval Team is aghast at Luffy's "Random Curry."</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While showing the newspaper to the rest of the team, Pedro assured a concerned Luffy that the story would have mentioned if a high-ranking member of the Revolutionary Army like <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Dragon</a> or <a href="/wiki/Sabo" title="Sabo">Sabo</a> had been captured or killed. After passing through a storm, Luffy presented his cooking, which his team found to be completely revolting and inedible. When Luffy admitted that he used up all the food they had, the team found themselves in a food shortage crisis.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marine_Rookie_Arc">Marine Rookie Arc</span></h4>
<p>After the team ran out of food, they began to get very hungry. However, Pedro spotted <a href="/wiki/Fron_Island" title="Fron Island">Fron Island</a> in the distance, and the team decided to go there to find food, even though Pekoms warned them that a <a href="/wiki/Marine" class="mw-redirect" title="Marine">Marine</a> base was located there. Pedro and Pekoms stayed behind to guard the Thousand Sunny while the others traveled to the island on the <a href="/wiki/Shark_Submerge_III" title="Shark Submerge III">Shark Submerge III</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A few hours later, the others returned to the Sunny with a massive food stockpile, but Pedro and Pekoms ate most of it in 10 minutes due to being left starving on the ship.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Arc">Whole Cake Island Arc</span></h4>
<p>A few days later, Pedro and the rest of the team were famished from the lack of food and overheated as they passed through boiling waters, but they were saved from starvation when Luffy managed to catch <a href="/wiki/Animal_Species/Whole_Cake_Island_Saga#Armored_Stonefish" title="Animal Species/Whole Cake Island Saga">a gigantic fish</a>. While Luffy suffered from severe food poisoning after eating the fish's toxic skin, Pedro and the others enjoyed a meal prepared by Nami using Sanji's recipe. After entering Big Mom's waters, they were approached by a ship belonging to <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">Germa 66</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The team was confronted by <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Yonji" title="Vinsmoke Yonji">Sanji's youngest brother</a>, who refused to give them an antidote for Luffy's poisoning despite their pleas. Pedro prepared to fight Yonji, but <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Reiju" title="Vinsmoke Reiju">Yonji's sister</a> intervened and cured Luffy. After deciding not to disrupt the wedding by fighting, the two groups parted ways.<sup id="cite_ref-c826_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c826-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Pedro_Stops_a_Mink.png/revision/latest?cb=20170430180753" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Stops a Mink" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="137" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pedro Stops a Mink.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Stops_a_Mink.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Pedro_Stops_a_Mink.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170430180753" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Pedro_Stops_a_Mink.png/revision/latest?cb=20170430180753" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Stops a Mink" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Pedro_Stops_a_Mink.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170430180753" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="137" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pedro Stops a Mink.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Stops_a_Mink.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Pedro_Stops_a_Mink.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170430180753" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pedro_Stops_a_Mink.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro stops a wolf mink from drawing attention to him.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The team docked at <a href="/wiki/Cacao_Island" title="Cacao Island">Cacao Island</a>, where Pedro and <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> donned disguises and accompanied Luffy and <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Chopper</a> onto the island. When Luffy and Chopper ate an entire cafe and were confronted by a policeman, Pedro prepared to use force to help them, but instead watched in shock as Luffy and Chopper were saved by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Pudding" title="Charlotte Pudding">Charlotte Pudding</a>. Upon being approached by a wolf mink who recognized him, Pedro told the mink that he was on vacation and asked him to keep quiet about his presence. Soon afterward, he and the rest of the team accompanied Pudding to another cafe, where she fed them.<sup id="cite_ref-c827_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c827-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Sanji Retrieval Team was shocked to learn that the woman they were conversing with was Sanji's betrothed. When Pudding panicked upon learning that they were the Straw Hats, Pedro quickly restrained her and held a sword to her throat, to Nami's chagrin. After calming down, Pedro and the team listened as Pudding explained more about the <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Family" title="Charlotte Family">Charlotte Family</a> and her thoughts about Sanji. Pedro suggested keeping Pudding bound and gagged to ensure that she would not report to Big Mom, but Pudding showed them a secret route to <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island" title="Whole Cake Island">Whole Cake Island</a> and told them where to meet her while promising to bring Sanji to them. The Sanji Retrieval Team left in a hurry when guards arrived for Pudding and quickly returned to the Thousand Sunny; to their surprise, Pekoms was nowhere to be found, and they found a message telling them to turn back.<sup id="cite_ref-c828_18-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c828-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c5/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png/revision/latest?cb=20160620215707" class="image"><img alt="Sanji Retrieval Team Battles a Centipede" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sanji Retrieval Team Battles a Centipede.png" data-image-key="Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c5/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160620215707" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c5/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png/revision/latest?cb=20160620215707" class="image"><img alt="Sanji Retrieval Team Battles a Centipede" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c5/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160620215707" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sanji Retrieval Team Battles a Centipede.png" data-image-key="Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c5/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160620215707" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Sanji Retrieval Team battles a giant centipede.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As they traveled on Pudding's route, Pedro spotted the next island, <a href="/wiki/Jam_Island" title="Jam Island">Jam Island</a>. After Carrot asked to take over lookout duty, Pedro went down to the deck. When Carrot saw grape-colored waters nearby, Pedro revealed that some of the islands have rivers of juice that flow into the ocean and admitted that he had been in Totto Land once before upon Nami noting his considerable knowledge of the area. Suddenly, the team was attacked by a giant sea centipede, which they began battling.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, the team battled a swarm of giant ants before getting trapped in a frozen sea of syrup as night fell. After Pedro revealed that this sea froze every night and unfroze the next day, they worked to unfreeze the sea as Pedro revealed that the giant ants had once eaten his own ship. When Luffy wondered what he did there in the past, Pedro explained how he had once traveled with Pekoms as a pirate and came to Totto Land searching for Poneglyphs before being defeated here. Pedro also stated that since Inuarashi and Nekomamushi showed Luffy the Road Poneglyph on Zou, they must believe that he could follow in Roger's footsteps, as he was the only other stranger to see it, and so they needed to acquire Big Mom's Road Poneglyph. When Pedro offered to sneak in and steal it while the others rescued Sanji, Luffy agreed to this proposal as the ants returned. The next day, the team reached Whole Cake Island, and Pedro revealed that the tallest cake on it is Big Mom's castle.<sup id="cite_ref-Pirate_5-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pirate-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c9/Brook_and_Pedro_Infiltrate_Sweet_City.png/revision/latest?cb=20170702072702" class="image"><img alt="Brook and Pedro Infiltrate Sweet City" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="154" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Brook and Pedro Infiltrate Sweet City.png" data-image-key="Brook_and_Pedro_Infiltrate_Sweet_City.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c9/Brook_and_Pedro_Infiltrate_Sweet_City.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170702072702" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c9/Brook_and_Pedro_Infiltrate_Sweet_City.png/revision/latest?cb=20170702072702" class="image"><img alt="Brook and Pedro Infiltrate Sweet City" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c9/Brook_and_Pedro_Infiltrate_Sweet_City.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170702072702" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="154" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Brook and Pedro Infiltrate Sweet City.png" data-image-key="Brook_and_Pedro_Infiltrate_Sweet_City.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c9/Brook_and_Pedro_Infiltrate_Sweet_City.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170702072702" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Brook_and_Pedro_Infiltrate_Sweet_City.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro and Brook discover that their every move is being traced as they infiltrate Sweet City.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After docking at the island, Pedro and Brook split from the group in the <a href="/wiki/Shark_Submerge_III" title="Shark Submerge III">Shark Submerge III</a> in order to infiltrate Big Mom's palace and acquire a copy of her Road Poneglyph. Pedro apologized to Luffy, as he had ended up needing Brook's assistance despite already offering to acquire a copy of the poneglyph alone.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, having infiltrated Sweet City, Pedro and Brook read a newspaper article stating that <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> reconsidered his decision to leave Big Mom's crew. Discovering Pudding with Tamago at a bridal boutique, Pedro and Brook learned that Big Mom and her crew were aware of the Sanji Retrieval Team's movements.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Soon afterward, Pedro and Brook hid themselves inside <a href="/wiki/Bisu_Bisu_no_Mi" title="Bisu Bisu no Mi">a biscuit soldier</a> and waited to be taken to Big Mom's castle.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Pedro and Brook managed to infiltrate the castle and hid inside the alcohol storehouse. After surveying the Room of Treasure with <a href="/wiki/Yomi_Yomi_no_Mi" title="Yomi Yomi no Mi">his spirit</a>, Brook saw how heavily guarded the poneglyphs were. Realizing that their chances of success were slim to none and that they would never have another chance like this even if they returned with the rest of the Straw Hats, Pedro and Brook planned to have Pedro act as a decoy.<sup id="cite_ref-Plan_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Plan-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/49/Pedro_Causes_a_Distraction.png/revision/latest?cb=20161205035349" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Causes a Distraction" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="146" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pedro Causes a Distraction.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Causes_a_Distraction.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/49/Pedro_Causes_a_Distraction.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161205035349" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/49/Pedro_Causes_a_Distraction.png/revision/latest?cb=20161205035349" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Causes a Distraction" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/49/Pedro_Causes_a_Distraction.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161205035349" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="146" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pedro Causes a Distraction.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Causes_a_Distraction.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/49/Pedro_Causes_a_Distraction.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161205035349" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pedro_Causes_a_Distraction.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro takes out several soldiers in the Whole Cake Chateau.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As planned, Pedro created a diversion to lead the guards away from Brook.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> He eliminated most of the security inside the Room of Treasure before running through the halls, where he caught Big Mom's soldiers off guard with his speed before cutting them down. Pedro then ran up a wall, past some soldiers shooting at him, and he threw a bomb at the soldiers before landing back on the floor and continuing running.<sup id="cite_ref-Blitz_38-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blitz-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Eventually, the <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land#Chess_Soldiers" title="Totto Land">Chess Soldiers</a> drove Pedro into an open courtyard, where he was confronted by Tamago. As Tamago reminisced about their past clashes and reminded him of how Big Mom stole 50 years of his natural lifespan, Pedro revealed that he was well aware of this and had no intention of returning to Zou.<sup id="cite_ref-Tamago_3-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tamago-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Pedro and Tamago fought while Pedro recalled the results of his first intrusion of Totto Land. When Tamago demanded to know why Pedro had returned despite his shortened lifespan, Pedro explained that he had done so for the Straw Hats, whom he believed would one day surpass him and Tamago while causing the world to transition into its "dawn", but clarified that he had no intention of dying until they had achieved their goals as he cut Tamago in half.<sup id="cite_ref-Fight_10-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fight-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Pedro_Defeats_Hiyoko.png/revision/latest?cb=20180123094143" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Defeats Hiyoko" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pedro Defeats Hiyoko.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Defeats_Hiyoko.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Pedro_Defeats_Hiyoko.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180123094143" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Pedro_Defeats_Hiyoko.png/revision/latest?cb=20180123094143" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Defeats Hiyoko" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Pedro_Defeats_Hiyoko.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180123094143" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pedro Defeats Hiyoko.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Defeats_Hiyoko.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Pedro_Defeats_Hiyoko.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180123094143" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pedro_Defeats_Hiyoko.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro defeats Hiyoko.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sometime during the battle, Chopper and Carrot called out to Pedro from a nearby mirror, surprising him, and they made a plan for Pedro to win the battle and escape. Using <a href="/wiki/Tama_Tama_no_Mi" title="Tama Tama no Mi">his Devil Fruit power</a>, Tamago evolved into Viscount Hiyoko, gaining a chicken beak and wings, and he attacked Pedro with two knives. However, Pedro quickly cut Hiyoko apart, and Hiyoko began to evolve into his next form, Count Niwatori. Pedro then set off a large collection of explosives in his jacket, causing a massive explosion that engulfed Niwatori and his soldiers. Chopper and Carrot then saved Pedro by pulling him into the <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a>, successfully executing their plan. He soon informed them of Nami and Luffy's capture as Chopper and Carrot prepared to search for their friends. Pedro was shocked at Carrot's drawing of them and even more so when the mirrors replied back to him telling them that Nami escaped and was with Jinbe.<sup id="cite_ref-c853_35-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c853-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The team later found Nami and Jinbe and pulled them into the Mirro-World. Jinbe revealed that he had decided to leave the Big Mom Pirates without spinning the roulette wheel, and Pedro commended him for doing so, recalling the time Zepo spun it. The team then went looking for Luffy, Sanji, and Brook.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Pedro's group located Brook inside Big Mom's bedroom, being held in her hands as she slept. After binding and gagging <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a> and <a href="/wiki/Diesel" title="Diesel">Diesel</a> to keep them from alerting Big Mom, the team witnessed Big Mom and her three <a href="/wiki/Homies" title="Homies">homies</a> attacking a fly. The team became terrified, wondering how they were supposed to save Brook. The team then made a skeletal lookalike of Brook, which they planned to use to make a stand-in for the real Brook. After Chopper and Carrot's unsuccessful attempts to retrieve Brook, Pedro tried next, but Big Mom started tossing and turning, forcing him to retreat. After Jinbe and Nami successfully rescued Brook, Pedro apologized to Brook for putting him in danger by sending him to a highly guarded room, but Brook replied that it was a once-in-a-lifetime chance, as they would be unlikely to succeed in reaching the poneglyphs again without fighting a full-scale war. The team was then surprised and amazed to see that Brook successfully acquired copies of the three poneglyphs, which were hidden inside his skull.<sup id="cite_ref-c855_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c855-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> The group searched for Sanji and Luffy, but none of the mirrors saw them inside the castle. Pedro listened as Jinbe explained that Pekoms was alive and safe but nearly died because of a plot he was involved in.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png/revision/latest?cb=20180304023006" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hat Pirates Meet Fire Tank Pirates" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Straw Hat Pirates Meet Fire Tank Pirates.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180304023006" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png/revision/latest?cb=20180304023006" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hat Pirates Meet Fire Tank Pirates" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180304023006" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Straw Hat Pirates Meet Fire Tank Pirates.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180304023006" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro at the meeting with the Fire Tank Pirates.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Pedro's group later contacted Luffy through a mirror shard and he was happy to hear that Sanji was with him. After Luffy told them his intention to ruin the wedding ceremony, Pedro listened as Jinbe explained more about <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a>, such as his backstory and him plotting against Big Mom. He continued listening as Jinbe proposed that Luffy form an alliance with Bege.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> The Sanji Retrieval Team went to the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Tank_Pirates" title="Fire Tank Pirates">Fire Tank Pirates</a>' hideout, where they cleaned up before meeting with Bege and his crew.<sup id="cite_ref-c858_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c858-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> As Bege explained his plan to kill Big Mom, Pedro listened attentively. The meeting adjourned once Bege finished going over the plan.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Bege transported the alliance members to the wedding inside his body. Before Bege walked into the wedding venue, Pedro was shown sleeping.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> After the wedding ceremony began, the team initially encountered a small problem when Jinbe had difficulty waking Luffy up. After they woke Luffy with food, the team went into the mirror world and prepared to charge into the venue.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Once they heard the signal, the team unleashed duplicates of Luffy into the venue, causing chaos at the ceremony. Once all the duplicates were released, the team charged in. When Luffy was immobilized by Katakuri, Pedro prepared to help Luffy, but Jinbe came to his aid first.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9b/Pedro_Clashes_With_Oven.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423082536" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Clashes With Oven" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="134" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pedro Clashes With Oven.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Clashes_With_Oven.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9b/Pedro_Clashes_With_Oven.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180423082536" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9b/Pedro_Clashes_With_Oven.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423082536" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Clashes With Oven" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9b/Pedro_Clashes_With_Oven.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180423082536" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="134" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pedro Clashes With Oven.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Clashes_With_Oven.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9b/Pedro_Clashes_With_Oven.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180423082536" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pedro_Clashes_With_Oven.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro clashes with Charlotte Oven.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Brook destroyed the picture of Carmel, Pedro was confronted by Oven, who used his Devil Fruit powers to transfer heat into Pedro's sword, making it too hot to touch. Pedro was later told by Bege to back up the Straw Hats as the latter initiated his assassination operation.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> As Katakuri went after Luffy, Pedro tried to fight him but the Sweet Commander managed to get past him.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> However, despite Katakuri's efforts, Luffy showed Carmel's broken portrait to Big Mom, causing her to start screaming. Pedro then quickly put on his earplugs.<sup id="cite_ref-c865_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c865-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Pedro watched as Bege, Vito, and Gotti fired their KX Launchers at Big Mom. However, Big Mom's scream detonated the rockets before they could reach her, shocking Pedro and his allies. With the assassination attempt a failure, Caesar flew into the venue with the escape mirror and Bege signaled the alliance members to retreat. Before they could escape into the mirror, Big Mom's scream shattered it, leaving them trapped in the venue. Pedro then watched Bege transforming into a giant fortress to save the alliance.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Pedro's group and the Vinsmoke Family then retreated inside the fortress. However, the alliance found themselves in a dire situation as the fortress came under attack by a furious Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> As Bege's fortress continued to suffer damage from Big Mom's attacks, Pedro listened to Bege as he came up with a plan to escape with Caesar's help.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Pedro remained inside Bege as turned back into human form and had Caesar carry him out of the venue. As the Big Mom Pirates hindered their escape, Luffy, Sanji, and the Vinsmoke Family were overwhelmed by the enemy. Pedro and Jinbe prepared to go out to assist them, but the Tamatebako dropped to the base of the Whole Cake Chateau and the bomb inside the chest exploded, causing the castle to topple over.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As the castle collapsed, Pedro's group, Bege's crew, and the Vinsmoke Family got away. Pedro's group and the Fire Tank Pirates rendezvous at the northwest part of Whole Cake Island, where Bege decided to part ways with the Straw Hats.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> After Brook and Chopper separated from the group to retrieve the Shark Submerge, the rest head for the Thousand Sunny. As they approached the Seducing Woods, they ran into King Baum. Nami then used part of Big Mom's vivre card to control King Baum and forced him to transport the fleeing team. However, before they reached the Seducing Woods, a crazed Big Mom (while riding on Zeus) caught up to them.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/22/Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png/revision/latest?cb=20170821042718" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hats Clash in the Seducing Woods" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Straw Hats Clash in the Seducing Woods.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/22/Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170821042718" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/22/Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png/revision/latest?cb=20170821042718" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hats Clash in the Seducing Woods" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/22/Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170821042718" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Straw Hats Clash in the Seducing Woods.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/22/Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170821042718" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Sanji Retrieval Team clashes with the Big Mom Pirates while trying to escape.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Using Napoleon in its sword form, Big Mom unleashed an air slash that cut off a part of King Baum. As Big Mom prepared to attack again, Nami diverted Zeus' attention by using thunderclouds, causing the cloud homie to veer off-course and drop Big Mom. When Pedro and his group reached the Seducing Woods, Big Mom ordered the tree homies to stop the Straw Hats, but King Baum charged through them. Pedro and his group were later forced to jump off King Baum when Prometheus attacked and burned King Baum for his betrayal.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> The team continued running, but the Big Mom Pirates caught up to them, and Pedro clashed with one of them. However, he was quickly pulled away by Jinbe to prevent the team from splitting up.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Zeus ate Nami's Weather Egg, causing it to expand greatly, and Nami used it to hit the Big Mom Pirates with a massive thunderbolt, which the Sanji Retrieval Team barely managed to outrun.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/63/Pedro_Attacks_Perospero.png/revision/latest?cb=20170904153436" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Attacks Perospero" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="271" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pedro Attacks Perospero.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Attacks_Perospero.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/63/Pedro_Attacks_Perospero.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170904153436" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/63/Pedro_Attacks_Perospero.png/revision/latest?cb=20170904153436" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Attacks Perospero" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/63/Pedro_Attacks_Perospero.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170904153436" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="271" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pedro Attacks Perospero.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Attacks_Perospero.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/63/Pedro_Attacks_Perospero.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170904153436" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pedro_Attacks_Perospero.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro takes on Perospero in an act of self-sacrifice.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Nami's attack left Big Mom laying at the bottom of a crater. To the Straw Hats' shock, Big Mom was barely affected and continued to move. She ate through the ground as she moved back up, and the team started running again. They were then approached by Pudding and Chiffon. After Chiffon requested Sanji's help in making a cake for Big Mom, Sanji readily agreed to assist them. Big Mom then got back on her feet and unleashed another devastating air slash, and the two groups parted ways with Sanji heading to Cacao Island with Pudding and Chiffon while Pedro and his group continued fleeing to the Thousand Sunny. Pudding used her Devil Fruit powers to send memories flooding into the souls in the homies, allowing the Straw Hats to make it to the coast without trouble.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> They ran toward the Sunny, and came into conflict with Perospero and Katakuri, who were onboard. Pedro told Carrot not to be flustered by these events, as he believed that the Straw Hats would bring about the dawn of the world. While standing on the coast, Perospero trapped the Sunny in candy. Pedro attempted a sneak attack on him, but Perospero managed to block the mink's strike before pinning him to the ground. However, Pedro lit up his bomb stash in his jacket, causing a massive explosion that engulfed both of them. Although Perospero survived the explosion, Pedro was nowhere to be seen, fulfilling his sacrifice to the Sanji Retrieval Team.<sup id="cite_ref-c877_12-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c877-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Legacy">Legacy</span></h3>
<p>Through Pedro's sacrifice, he was successful in helping the Straw Hats escape Whole Cake Island. Wanting to honor Pedro's self sacrifice, Pekoms betrayed the Big Mom Pirates in his attempt to help Luffy escape Cacao Island after his victory against Katakuri inside the Mirro-World. After the Straw Hats escaped Totto Land, Sanji learned of his sacrifice and, recalling the time he first met him, mourned his death while silently blaming himself over his death.
</p><p>A grave was erected for Pedro near Amigasa Village in <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">Kuri</a> region.<sup id="cite_ref-c955_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c955-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Eventually upon learning of his subordinate's death, <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a> was pleased to hear how Pedro died for a noble cause that allowed the Sanji Retrieval Team to reach Wano. Nekomamushi later personally fought Perospero to avenge Pedro, and ultimately succeeded by defeating Perospero with his <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a> form.<sup id="cite_ref-c1026_26-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1026-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" /> When Luffy fought Kaidou, Luffy cites Pedro as one of the people he must win for, alongside <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Tama" title="Kurozumi Tama">Kurozumi Tama</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kozuki_Momonosuke" class="mw-redirect" title="Kozuki Momonosuke">Kozuki Momonosuke</a>, which allows him to get back into <a href="/wiki/Gear_5" class="mw-redirect" title="Gear 5">Gear 5</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span></h2>
<p>During the escape from Whole Cake Island in the anime, Pedro defeated Kato in the Seducing Woods.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> In the manga, the entire pursuit squad was defeated by Nami using Zeus' thunderbolt.
</p>
